Eze 16:22 (vc=65985 — VCG-05): "in all your abominations and your whorings you did not remember the days of your youth" — the failure to remember (a cognitive-memorial function) is associated with abomination. Eze 20:4 (vc=65994 — VCG-05): "let them know the abominations of their fathers" — a cognitive declaration requiring understanding. Eze 8:17 (vc=65980 — VCG-05): "is it too light a thing for the house of Judah to commit the abominations that they commit here" — the cognitive assessment of gravity has failed: they consider abomination a trivial matter, showing a mind that has lost the capacity to assess the gravity of idolatrous acts.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Yes. Mind-location is directly evidenced through the thought-vocabulary. Isa 59:7 (vc=38203 — VCG-02): "their thoughts are thoughts of iniquity" — the thought-life itself is the explicit site. Jer 4:14 (vc=38205 — VCG-02): "How long shall your wicked thoughts lodge within you?" — thoughts of iniquity lodge in the mind as persistent inner tenants. Isa 55:7 (vc=38200 — VCG-02): "the unrighteous man his thoughts" that must be forsaken — the thoughts are the specific location of the unrighteous man's iniquity. Eze 11:2 (vc=38193 — VCG-02): "men who devise iniquity and who give wicked counsel" — devising is an explicitly cognitive act of deliberate mental planning.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Yes. Jude 10 (vc=14355 — VCG-01) directly evidences the cognitive/mind dimension: "these people blaspheme all that they do not understand, and they are destroyed by all that they, like unreasoning animals, understand instinctively." The cognitive faculty is explicitly named through its failure: they blaspheme what they do not understand — the mind's comprehension function has failed or been bypassed, and contempt fills the void. The contrast between "understand instinctively" (pre-cognitive animal-level) and not-understanding (failed rational comprehension) directly locates the characteristic in the cognitive dimension of the inner person.

---

##### T2.4.2 — What does mind-location reveal — what aspect of the mind's function (thought, discernment, understanding) does this characteristic engage?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

Mind-location reveals that wickedness-as-settled-person-identity engages and corrupts the deliberative and perceptive functions of the mind. The deliberative corruption is most visible in Pro 12:5 (deceptive counsels), Job 21:16 (morally alien counsel-frame), and Isa 5:23 (VCG-05 — the corrupt judicial mind that acquits the guilty for a bribe). The perceptive corruption is visible in Pro 4:19 (blindness to what causes stumbling), Dan 12:10 (the wicked "cannot understand" in the eschatological refining process), and Isa 26:10 ("does not see the majesty of the Lord"). The mind-location reveals that wickedness corrupts not only what the person chooses but what they can perceive and reason about — the characteristic progressively disables the cognitive apparatus through which moral reality would otherwise be apprehended.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

Mind-location reveals that evil as constitutional inner nature engages and corrupts the cognitive functions of understanding and discernment. Col 1:21 (vc=14424 — VCG-06) names the mind as "hostile" — the relational-cognitive orientation of the mind is the point of corruption. 1Ti 6:4 (vc=14470 — VCG-06) shows the mind as "devoid of understanding" when inflated with conceit — the characteristic occupies the cognitive space where understanding should reside, producing evil suspicions in its place. The mind-location reveals the characteristic corrupting two mind functions: the evaluative-relational function (making the mind hostile to others) and the epistemic function (replacing understanding with evil suspicions). The mind-location is secondary to the heart-location but directly evidenced.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Mind-location reveals that abomination specifically engages the deliberative-planning function of the mind. Pro 15:26 (vc=1679 — VCG-02) targets "thoughts" (machashevot) — deliberate planned thought rather than involuntary passing cognition. The wicked person's deliberate moral reasoning is itself an abomination. The cognitive failure of Isa 44:19 (vc=65961 — VCG-05) — "no one considers" — reveals that the absence of reflective moral cognition enables abomination: the person who does not stop to consider what they are doing proceeds into abomination through cognitive abdication. Mind-location shows the characteristic engaging the evaluative-deliberative mind rather than mere perceptual cognition.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Mind-location reveals that idolatrous abomination corrupts the cognitive-evaluative function that assesses gravity. Eze 8:17 (vc=65980 — VCG-05): treating abomination as a light thing shows that the evaluative cognitive faculty — the capacity to assess moral and spiritual weight — has been dulled. The characteristic also suppresses the memory function: Eze 16:22 (vc=65985 — VCG-05) — not remembering origins; Eze 16:43 (vc=65987 — VCG-05) — failure to remember youth. The mind-location reveals the characteristic as corrupting specifically the evaluative and memorial cognitive functions — the person can no longer correctly assess the gravity of what they do or recall the covenantal history that should check their idolatrous attachment.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Mind-location reveals that iniquity as active scheming engages the deliberative-planning function of the mind — specifically the capacity for premeditated scheming and devising. Mic 2:1 (vc=38217 — VCG-02): "those who devise wickedness and work evil on their beds" — the devising is nocturnal planning, using the quiet of the night for deliberate mental scheming. Eze 11:2 (vc=38193 — VCG-02): "devise iniquity and give wicked counsel" — the cognitive-planning function produces both the inner scheme and the social counsel that extends it. Isa 59:7 (vc=38203 — VCG-02): "thoughts are thoughts of iniquity" — the thought-life is entirely colonised by iniquitous content. The mind-location reveals the characteristic as one that specifically co-opts the deliberative-planning faculty — the mind's highest-level cognitive function — for the production of evil.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Jude 10 (vc=14355 — VCG-01) reveals that the characteristic specifically engages the mind's comprehension-and-discernment function — but through its failure. The characteristic fills the gap left by absent understanding with contemptuous speech: what is not understood is blasphemed rather than humbly acknowledged as unknown. The mind's discernment function (the capacity to accurately recognise and assess what one encounters) has been bypassed — replaced by the instinctual level of unreasoning animals. Mind-location reveals the characteristic as a cognitive-regressive phenomenon: it operates below the level of rational discernment, expressing itself through contempt where understanding should be.

---

##### T2.4.3 — If the evidence is silent on mind-location, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The evidence is not silent; mind-location is evidenced (T2.4.1–T2.4.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

Mind-location is evidenced (T2.4.1–T2.4.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Mind-location is evidenced (T2.4.1–T2.4.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Mind-location is evidenced (T2.4.1–T2.4.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Mind-location is richly evidenced (T2.4.1–T2.4.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Mind-location is evidenced via Jude 10 (vc=14355 — VCG-01) (T2.4.1–T2.4.2). This prompt is satisfied.

---

#### T2.5 — Other Soul Subsets

##### T2.5.1 — Does the verse evidence surface any soul-level location beyond heart and mind for this characteristic?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The evidence surfaces "way" (derek) as a directional-volitional location beyond heart and mind — it names the person's overall trajectory and life-direction. This is the VCG-07 corpus's dominant language: "his wicked way" (Eze 3:18; 33:8; 33:11; Isa 55:7; Pro 4:14). While "way" is not a faculty but a directional concept, it describes the totality of the person's volitional thrust — which in the programme's framework is a soul-level phenomenon. The eyes also appear in Pro 21:4 (VCG-03): "haughty eyes and a proud heart, the lamp of the wicked, are sin" — the eyes as the vehicle of pride's inner disposition expressing outward. Beyond this, the "belly" (Pro 13:25) as the seat of insatiable appetite is a sub-soul location in the Hebrew anthropological tradition.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

Yes. The conscience (syneidēsis) is explicitly evidenced as a location of this characteristic. Heb 10:22 (vc=14426 — VCG-06): "hearts sprinkled clean from an evil conscience" — the conscience is named as a location where evil constitutionally resides, and its "evil" state makes approach to God impossible. The conscience is the specific faculty named in Heb 10:22 as the primary barrier between the constitutionally evil inner person and the holy God. The whole-body/whole-person framing of Mat 6:23 (vc=14458 — VCG-03 — "your whole body will be full of darkness") implies the characteristic is not localised to a single faculty but permeates the whole inner person.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Yes. The conscience is the most significant additional constitutional locus. VCG-04 (11 verses) is entirely devoted to the conscience's relationship with abomination across its states — wholly silenced (Jer 6:15; Jer 8:12), grieving and active (Eze 9:4), callable to repentance (Eze 14:6), awakened to produce self-loathing (Eze 36:31), bearing permanent shame (Eze 44:13), and rebelling (Eze 44:6). The conscience as a distinct inner faculty is the most extensively evidenced constitutional locus beyond heart and mind in this characteristic. Additionally, Pro 13:19 (vc=1687 — VCG-05) evidences the soul's desire faculty as a locus (T2.2.1).

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Yes. The eyes (as the perceptive-desire faculty) are explicitly evidenced. Eze 20:7 (vc=1634 — VCG-05): "the detestable things your eyes feast on" — the eyes are the perceptive-desire faculty through which idolatrous attachment is sustained and fed. Eze 20:8 (vc=65911 — VCG-05): "none of them cast away the detestable things their eyes feasted on" — the eyes' feasting habit is the mechanism of the characteristic's perpetuation. Eze 6:9 (vc=1697 — VCG-05): "eyes that go whoring after their idols" — the eyes are specifically named as going whoring, paralleling the heart's whoring. The eyes in this context are not merely physical organs but the inner-perceptive faculty of desire — the capacity for morally-weighted visual attention that feeds the soul's attachment.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Yes. The tongue/mouth as the expressive-concealment faculty is directly evidenced. Psa 10:7 (vc=38225 — VCG-04): "under his tongue are mischief and iniquity" — the iniquity is located beneath the tongue as a hidden reservoir. This is an inner-sub-set location: the tongue/mouth as the site where iniquity waits for deployment. Additionally, Isa 58:9 (vc=38201 — VCG-04): "speaking wickedness" — the vocal-expressive faculty is named as a location of iniquitous expression. These tongue-mouth references are expressive-concealment locations: iniquity stored beneath the tongue ready to flow outward.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Yes. Jude 8 (vc=14354 — VCG-01) evidences the volitional faculty as a distinct constitutional location: "relying on their dreams, they defile the flesh, reject authority, and blaspheme the glorious ones." The will (rejection of authority) is the constitutional location of the characteristic's source. Additionally, the body's speech-instruments are specifically named: Rev 13:6 (vc=14356 — VCG-01): "opened its mouth to utter blasphemies" — the mouth as the body's speech-instrument is the constitutional locus through which the characteristic becomes operative. The will (refusing, rejecting) and the mouth (uttering) are the two additional constitutional locations beyond heart and mind in this corpus.

---

##### T2.5.2 — If so, what is that location, and what does it reveal?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The "way" (derek) as directional-volitional location reveals that wickedness-as-settled-person-identity is not merely an interior state but an entire life-orientation — the person's direction of travel as a whole. This is analytically important: it means the characteristic is not localised to a discrete faculty but has organised the entire person's movement through life. The "belly" location (Pro 13:25) reveals that wickedness operates at the level of basic appetite — the person's most fundamental need-structure is corrupted (their hunger is perpetually unsatisfied by evil, which cannot nourish). The "eyes" location (Pro 21:4 — haughty eyes) reveals that wickedness occupies even the perceptive-relational faculty by which one relates to others and assesses one's own relative position.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The conscience location (Heb 10:22 — VCG-06) reveals that evil as constitutional inner nature occupies the specifically relational-moral faculty — the conscience that should mediate between the person and God, making approach possible. When the conscience is constitutionally evil ("an evil conscience"), it does not function as a clear channel for approach to God but as a barrier. This reveals the characteristic's most profound relational consequence: it corrupts the very faculty (conscience) whose designed function is to enable the human person's access to God. The characteristic in the conscience is the characteristic at its most theologically consequential location.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The conscience location (VCG-04, 11V) reveals that abomination has a specific and privileged relationship with the conscience as the inner-being faculty designed to register moral violations and produce the appropriate shame-response. The conscience's normal function in relation to abomination is grief and shame: Eze 9:4 (vc=1698 — VCG-04): grieving; Eze 36:31 (vc=1681 — VCG-04): self-loathing upon restored memory. When the conscience is functional, it registers abomination. When it is silenced (Jer 6:15; 8:12 — VCG-04), the abomination proceeds without inner check. The conscience location reveals the characteristic as one whose normal inner-being containment mechanism is specifically the shame-producing conscience — and whose most dangerous form is when that mechanism has been rendered inoperative.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The eyes-as-perceptive-desire faculty (Eze 20:7 — VCG-05; Eze 6:9 — VCG-05) reveal that idolatrous abomination operates through a sustained visual-desire loop: the eyes feast on the detestable things, feeding the soul's attachment to them, which directs the heart further toward them. This is a distinct inner-being mechanism: perception feeding desire feeding attachment feeding further perception. The character of the shiq.quts (idol-objects as things the eyes feast on) shows that the idolatrous objects are presented as attractive to the perceptive faculty — the visual-desire loop is a specific mechanism through which idolatrous attachment deepens.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The tongue-as-location (Psa 10:7 — VCG-04: "under his tongue are mischief and iniquity") reveals that iniquity has a specific concealment-deployment mechanism within the inner person. Iniquity is not only stored in the heart but positioned under the tongue — the speech-faculty's anteroom — ready to be released as harmful speech (cursing, deceit, oppression in the same verse: "his mouth is filled with cursing and deceit and oppression"). This tongue-location reveals the characteristic as having a built-in social delivery mechanism: it generates inwardly (heart-mind), stores sub-lingually, and deploys outwardly through speech. The tongue-location is thus the constitutional bridge between the inner scheming and the outer harm.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

The will-location (Jude 8 — VCG-01) reveals that the characteristic's inner source is volitional rather than merely cognitive or affective: the authority-rejection is an act of will that precedes and enables the blasphemous expression. The mouth-location (Rev 13:6 — VCG-01) reveals the characteristic as constitutively embodied in its expression: the mouth is the necessary instrument through which inner wickedness becomes socially operative blasphemy. These two locations — inner will (source) and mouth/speech-instrument (expression) — define the characteristic's constitutional range: it spans from the deepest volitional-inner level to the body's speech-expressing surface.

---

##### T2.5.3 — If the evidence is silent, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The evidence is not silent; additional soul-sub-set locations are identified (T2.5.1–T2.5.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The evidence is not silent; conscience location is evidenced (T2.5.1–T2.5.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Additional constitutional locations beyond heart and mind are evidenced (T2.5.1–T2.5.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Additional soul-sub-set locations are evidenced (T2.5.1–T2.5.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Additional soul-level locations are evidenced (T2.5.1–T2.5.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Additional constitutional locations (will, mouth) are evidenced (T2.5.1–T2.5.2). This prompt is satisfied.

---

#### T2.6 — Body — Significance

##### T2.6.1 — Does the verse evidence link this characteristic to a specific body part?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

Yes. The evidence links wickedness-as-settled-person-identity to multiple body parts as expressive instruments. The mouth is the most prominent: Pro 10:6 and 10:11 ("the mouth of the wicked conceals violence"), Pro 10:32 ("the mouth of the wicked knows what is perverse"), Pro 11:11 ("by the mouth of the wicked [a city] is overthrown"), Pro 12:6, 15:28, 19:28 — the wicked person's mouth is the primary body-level marker. The arm/hand appears in Psa 10:15 (VCG-05 — "break the arm of the wicked"), Eze 7:21 (VCG-03 — the wicked used as instruments of plunder — their "hand"), Job 38:15 ("their uplifted arm is broken"). The "feet" / "path" are implied in Psa 1:1 (walking in counsel) and Pro 4:14 (entering the path). Pro 21:4: "haughty eyes and a proud heart" — the eyes carry the expression of inner pride.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

Yes. The eye and the mouth are the primary body-part links. Eye: Mat 6:23 (vc=14458 — VCG-03): "if your eye is bad, your whole body will be full of darkness" — the eye as the body part through which the constitutional inner evil expresses its perceptive corruption. Mouth: Mat 12:34 (vc=14419 — VCG-03): "out of the abundance of the heart the mouth speaks" — the mouth as the expressive instrument of the heart-treasury of evil. Luk 6:45 (vc=14421 — VCG-03): the same mouth-as-overflow-of-heart-treasury pattern. 3Jo 10 (vc=14454 — VCG-04): "talking wicked nonsense against us" — the mouth as the instrument of domineering inner malice. Body members in general: Rom 6:13 (vc=14340 — VCG-06): "do not present your members to sin as instruments for unrighteousness" — the body's members as potential instruments for the constitutional unrighteousness.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Yes. Multiple body parts appear. Lips: Pro 8:7 (vc=65953 — VCG-02): "wickedness is an abomination to my lips" — Wisdom's lips are the body part that expresses the divine faculty of moral revulsion; Pro 12:22 (vc=65955 — VCG-02): "lying lips are an abomination to the Lord" — the lips as the instrument of deceptive speech that is abominable. Ear: Pro 28:9 (vc=65958 — VCG-03): "if one turns away his ear from hearing the law" — the ear as the faculty of receptive hearing is the body part whose turning away renders prayer abominable. Forehead: Rev 17:5 (vc=65878 — VCG-05): the name of abomination written on the forehead — the forehead as the site of public identity disclosure. Face: Eze 14:6 (vc=65984 — VCG-04): "turn away your faces from all your abominations" — the face as the direction-of-orientation indicator.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Yes. Eyes and hands are the primary body parts. Eyes: Eze 20:7 (vc=1634 — VCG-05): "the detestable things your eyes feast on"; Eze 6:9 (vc=1697 — VCG-05): "eyes that go whoring after their idols." Hands (implied through craftsmanship and installation): Eze 7:20 (vc=65909 — VCG-05): "His beautiful ornament they used for pride, and they made their abominable images and their detestable things of it" — making with hands; Deu 29:17 (vc=65897 — VCG-02): "idols of wood and stone, of silver and gold" — crafted objects. Mouth/teeth: Zec 9:7 (vc=65918 — VCG-04): "I will take away its blood from its mouth, and its abominations from between its teeth" — abominations lodged in the mouth as physical-metaphorical location. The installation of idols in sacred space (Jer 7:30 — vc=65904 — VCG-04; Jer 32:34 — vc=65907 — VCG-04) implies bodily agency (hands placing).

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Yes. Multiple body parts appear. Hand: Job 11:14 (vc=38207 — VCG-04): "if iniquity is in your hand, put it far away" — iniquity located in the hand as the active-agency instrument. Isa 59:6 (vc=38202 — VCG-04): "deeds of violence are in their hands" — the hand as the body part where iniquity's deeds reside. Tongue/mouth: Psa 10:7 (vc=38225 — VCG-04): "under his tongue are mischief and iniquity"; Pro 6:12 (vc=38223 — VCG-03): "goes about with crooked speech." Feet: Isa 59:7 (vc=38203 — VCG-02): "their feet run to evil" — the feet as the body part through which the will's eager movement toward iniquity is expressed; Pro 6:18 (vc=38224 — VCG-02): "feet that make haste to run to evil." Face/heart juxtaposition: Psa 28:3 (vc=38232 — VCG-03): "speak peace" (face/mouth) while "evil is in their hearts" — the face/outward expression vs. heart/inner condition.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Yes. The mouth is the primary body part. Rev 13:6 (vc=14356 — VCG-01): "opened its mouth to utter blasphemies against God" — the mouth as the body's primary speech-instrument is explicitly named as the vehicle through which the characteristic operates. The opening of the mouth is the act through which inner defiant contempt becomes operative blasphemy. The entire characteristic is constitutively mouth-mediated: evil must be "expressed through speech" — the speech-faculty, located in the mouth, is the necessary constitutional bridge between inner wickedness and its social expression.

---

##### T2.6.2 — If so, what is Scripture doing by making that link — is it emphatic, functional, expressive, indicative, or mediating?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The mouth-link (the dominant body connection) is primarily expressive and indicative: the wicked person's speech reveals and enacts the inner orientation. The mouth does not cause wickedness — it discloses and extends it outward into social space (Pro 12:6: "lie in wait for blood" — the words as instruments; Pro 10:6: "conceals violence" — the mouth masking and enabling). The arm/hand link is functional and mediating: the wicked person's capacity for harm is located in their physical power (Psa 10:15 — "break the arm" = dismantle their harm-capacity; Job 38:15 — "their uplifted arm is broken" = divine termination of their agency). The eyes link (Pro 21:4) is expressive and indicative: haughty eyes display the inner pride that constitutes the wicked person's characteristic orientation. The body-links are consistently diagnostic (displaying inner character) and instrumental (enacting inner orientation outward).

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The eye-link (Mat 6:23 — VCG-03) is indicative and functional: the eye's moral state (bad vs. good) is indicative of the whole inner person's condition, and functionally it is the perceptive channel through which inner darkness is spread to the whole body. Scripture's use here is diagnostic — the quality of the eye reveals and expresses the constitutional inner condition. The mouth-link (Mat 12:34; Luk 6:45 — VCG-03) is expressive and revelatory: the mouth does not cause the constitutional evil but reveals and enacts it. Scripture is using the mouth as the diagnostic instrument — what overflows from the mouth reveals the state of the heart-treasury. The body-members link (Rom 6:13 — VCG-06) is functional-mediating: the body's members are the means through which constitutional unrighteousness is enacted outward in the world; the link is about instrumentality.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The lip-links (Pro 8:7; Pro 12:22 — VCG-02) are expressive and indicative: the lips reveal and enact the inner character — lying lips disclose a heart of deception. The ear-link (Pro 28:9 — VCG-03) is functional and mediating: the ear's turning away from the law is the volitional act that corrupts the worship relationship, making prayer abominable. The function here is the reverse of the normal: the ear should mediate receptivity to divine instruction; its deliberate turning away mediates the corruption of the person's access to God. The forehead-link (Rev 17:5 — VCG-05) is emphatic and identifying: public disclosure of inner identity. The face-link (Eze 14:6 — VCG-04) is directional and indicative: the face shows the direction the person is oriented; turning the face from abominations is the commanded inner-volitional act expressed through the body's directional faculty.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The eyes-link (Eze 20:7; 6:9 — VCG-05) is expressive and functional: the eyes as the body's perceptive-desire faculty express the inner attachment to idolatrous objects; they also function as the mechanism through which the characteristic deepens (feasting on the idols feeds the inner attachment). The link is both diagnostic and causal: the eyes reveal the inner state and contribute to its perpetuation. The hands-link (making idols from beautiful ornament — Eze 7:20 — VCG-05) is expressive and mediating: the bodily act of craft production enacts the inner idolatrous disposition outward. The mouth/teeth-link (Zec 9:7 — VCG-04) is emphatic and vivid: abominations lodged in the mouth/teeth show how thoroughly the characteristic has penetrated the physical person, requiring divine extraction.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Three distinct functions are evidenced. The hand-link (Job 11:14 — VCG-04) is functional and expressive: the hand as the instrument of agency; iniquity in the hand is the inner condition enacted through the body's primary work-instrument. The commanded response ("put it far away") shows the hand-link as indicating active-enactment requiring volitional reversal. The tongue/mouth-link (Psa 10:7 — VCG-04) is concealment-deployment: the iniquity hidden beneath the tongue is positioned for strategic release through speech; Scripture's naming of the sub-lingual location is emphatic — the evil is not merely in the abstract inner life but positioned in the speech mechanism. The feet-link (Isa 59:7 — VCG-02; Pro 6:18 — VCG-02) is directional-indicative: feet running to evil shows the whole embodied person moving eagerly toward iniquity — the eagerness of the body's locomotion reveals the will's inner orientation.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Rev 13:6 (vc=14356 — VCG-01): "opened its mouth to utter blasphemies" — the mouth-link is functional and mediating: the mouth is the specific constitutional instrument through which the beast's inner defiant contempt becomes social reality. The mouth-link is not merely emphatic (this is how it works) but constitutive (without the mouth, the inner evil cannot become operative blasphemy). The deliberate "opened its mouth" also reveals agency and intention: the mouth is not involuntarily venting but deliberately opened — the volitional act of opening the mouth is part of the characteristic's inner-being operation. The mouth functions as both mediating instrument and indicator of deliberate agency.

---

##### T2.6.3 — If no body-part link is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

Body-part links are evidenced (T2.6.1–T2.6.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

Body-part links are evidenced (T2.6.1–T2.6.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Body-part links are evidenced (T2.6.1–T2.6.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Body-part links are evidenced (T2.6.1–T2.6.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Body-part links are evidenced (T2.6.1–T2.6.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

A body-part link (mouth) is evidenced (T2.6.1–T2.6.2). This prompt is satisfied.

---

#### T2.7 — Body — Direction

##### T2.7.1 — Where a body-characteristic link exists, which direction does it run — does the soul express through the body, does the body feed back to the soul, or does it run in both directions?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The direction is consistently from soul outward to body: the inner orientation of wickedness (soul, heart, will) expresses itself through the body's instruments (mouth, arm, eyes). Pro 12:6 ("the words of the wicked lie in wait for blood") evidences the soul-to-mouth directionality — the inner lethal intent flows outward through speech. Psa 36:1 (VCG-02) supports this: the transgression-voice operates "deep in his heart" first, then surfaces in the person's outward conduct and absence of fear. The body does not generate wickedness — it enacts and reveals it. There is one partial exception: Pro 5:22 ("ensnared by the cords of his sin") suggests a feedback loop — the wickedness the body enacts (acts of sin) generates constraints that deepen the inner condition. But this is a consequence-loop, not a primary body-to-soul causation.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The direction runs consistently from the inner constitutional condition outward to the body's expressive instruments. Mat 12:34 (vc=14419 — VCG-03): the heart's abundance flows to the mouth — inner to outer. Mat 6:23 (vc=14458 — VCG-03): the bad eye floods the "whole body" — a secondary inner-to-outer direction (the eye as the inner-perceptive faculty expressing outward through the body's illumination). Rom 6:13 (vc=14340 — VCG-06): the body's members become instruments for the unrighteousness — the inner condition uses the body as its channel outward. The constitutional evil (inner) → body members (outer) direction is entirely consistent across the corpus. There is no evidence of a body-feeding-back-to-soul direction in this corpus.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The direction is consistently from inner constitutional condition outward to the body's expressive and receptive instruments. The lying lips (Pro 12:22 — VCG-02) express an inner character of deception — the inner condition flows to the lips. Wisdom's lips that find wickedness abominable (Pro 8:7 — VCG-02) express an inner moral faculty of revulsion outward through speech. The ear turned from the law (Pro 28:9 — VCG-03) is the volitional inner act of rejection expressed through the body's receptive faculty — but here a nuance: the ear's turning away from the law also functions as the mechanism through which the inner person is closed to divine instruction, so there is a secondary body-to-inner feedback: deliberate ear-closing reinforces the inner closure. The face-turning of Eze 14:6 (VCG-04) is directional — the face expresses the inner orientation's direction and is also the commanded instrument of volitional redirection.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The direction is bidirectional but with the primary flow from inner to outer. Primary inner-to-outer: the inner attachment of heart and soul to idols → the eyes feast on them → the hands craft them → they are installed in sacred space. The inner devotional commitment expresses itself through the body's perceptive (eyes), productive (hands), and locative (installation) acts. Secondary outer-to-inner (feedback): the sustained feeding of the eyes on the idolatrous objects reinforces and deepens the inner attachment — Eze 20:8 (vc=65911 — VCG-05): "none of them cast away the detestable things their eyes feasted on" — the sustained visual-desire habit reinforces the inner attachment. The body-characteristic link runs in both directions here: inner desire → bodily feasting → reinforced inner desire, creating a self-perpetuating loop.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The primary direction is inner-to-outer: the inner scheming (heart-mind devising) → expressive through body parts (hand enacting, feet running, tongue deploying). Mic 2:1 (vc=38217 — VCG-02): "devise wickedness on their beds; when the morning dawns, they perform it" — the inner nocturnal devising flows outward through bodily enactment at dawn. Isa 59:7 (vc=38203 — VCG-02): "thoughts are thoughts of iniquity" → "feet run to evil" — the cognitive inner state directly drives the bodily directional movement. Pro 6:18 (vc=38224 — VCG-02): "heart devises wicked plans" → "feet make haste to run to evil" — same inner-to-outer sequence. Secondary feedback (outer-to-inner): Pro 19:28 (vc=38220 — VCG-03): "the mouth of the wicked devours iniquity" — the bodily act of devouring iniquity through speech feeds back into the inner appetite, reinforcing it.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

The direction runs primarily inner-to-outer: inner will-wickedness → volitional choice to open the mouth → speech-act through the mouth → social/relational impact. Rev 13:6 (vc=14356 — VCG-01): the beast's mouth utters what originates in the inner orientation of defiant contempt. Rev 16:9 (vc=14352 — VCG-01): the inner will that refuses to repent finds expression through the cursing speech act. The sequence is consistently inner-to-outer. There is also a possible feedback dimension: the act of cursing God's name under judgment (Rev 16:9/11/21 — VCG-01) does not reduce but deepens the will's defiance — the very act of expressing blasphemy through the mouth appears to reinforce and deepen the inner hardened state rather than relieving it.

---

##### T2.7.2 — What is the consequence of that directionality for understanding the characteristic?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The soul-to-body directionality means that the characteristic cannot be addressed at the body level alone — the body's expressions (speech, action, eyes) are symptoms rather than causes. This is analytically confirmed by the Ezekiel corpus (VCG-07): the call to turn is addressed to the inner person's "way" and "will" (Eze 18:21 — "turns away from all his sins and does what is just and right"), not primarily to bodily behaviour as the point of address. Behavioural change is the evidence of inner turning (Eze 33:15 — "restores the pledge, gives back what he has taken by robbery") but the inner turn is the cause. The directionality also means that the body becomes a measure of the inner character's state — examining the wicked person's speech (VCG-08) reveals the inner orientation (Pro 12:6: "the words of the wicked lie in wait for blood").

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The consistently inner-to-outer directionality means that addressing the body's expressions (stopping the mouth, controlling the eye) without addressing the constitutional inner condition is insufficient. Mat 12:34 (vc=14419 — VCG-03) makes this explicit: you cannot speak good "when you are evil" — the mouth's output is determined by the heart's state, not by behavioural self-control. Luk 11:39 (vc=14407 — VCG-05) exposes the same issue: the Pharisees clean the outside but the inside remains full of greed and wickedness — external cleansing does not address the constitutional inner condition. The directionality establishes that transformation must begin at the constitutional inner level (heart, conscience, mind) for the body's expressions to genuinely change.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The primarily inner-to-outer direction means that addressing the body's expressions (controlling the lips, physically opening the ear) without addressing the inner constitutional condition is insufficient. Luk 16:15 (vc=21 — VCG-02) makes this explicit in the NT register: "God knows your hearts" — the divine verdict on abomination bypasses all outward expression and goes directly to the inner constitutional condition. The Pharisees who exalt themselves before men (outward social performance) are still abominable in God's sight because the heart-level pride remains. The directionality establishes that abomination's address requires transformation at the heart/conscience level, not merely behavioural or speech-level correction. The secondary ear-to-inner feedback (Pro 28:9) suggests that deliberate bodily acts of reception (opening the ear to God's law) do have inner consequences, but the primary causation remains inner-to-outer.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The bidirectional character of the body-characteristic link means that the physical environment of idolatrous objects (the installed idols, the visible detestable things) actively reinforces and deepens the inner attachment. This is confirmed by the Deuteronomic reform strategy (VCG-02): Deu 7:25 (vc=1682 — VCG-02): "you shall burn with fire" — the physical destruction of the idol-objects removes the visual-desire feedback loop. 2Ch 34:33 (vc=65946 — VCG-03): Josiah's removal of all abominations from the territory enabled the people to "not turn away from following the Lord" — removing the physical objects removed their reinforcing influence on the inner attachment. The bidirectionality establishes that addressing idolatrous abomination requires both inner transformation (the heart turning) and physical removal of the outer idol-objects (the feedback mechanism).

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The primarily inner-to-outer direction means that external behavioural control without inner address is insufficient — the scheming continues internally even if constrained externally. Jer 4:14 (vc=38205 — VCG-02): "wash your heart from evil" — the required address is inner (wash the heart), not merely behavioural. The secondary outer-to-inner feedback (mouth devouring iniquity — Pro 19:28 — VCG-03) reveals that speech habits reinforce the inner appetite, making the characteristic self-perpetuating through its own expressive channels. The directionality establishes that addressing iniquity requires inner transformation at the heart/thought level and management of the expressive channels that feed back into it.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

The primarily inner-to-outer direction means that addressing the speech output without transforming the inner will is insufficient — the characteristic's source is the will's hardened defiance (Rev 16:9/11/21 — VCG-01), and only transformation at the will level (repentance) would address it. Rev 16:9 (VCG-01): "they did not repent" — the non-addressed inner will continues generating blasphemous speech regardless of external judgment. The secondary feedback (speaking blasphemy deepens the will's hardening) means that the act of expressing evil through speech is not merely symptomatic but formative: the characteristic reinforces itself through its own expression. Addressing evil speech requires inner will-transformation (repentance), not merely speech-management.

---

##### T2.7.3 — If no body-characteristic link is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

Body-characteristic links and their directionality are evidenced (T2.7.1–T2.7.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

Body-characteristic links and their directionality are evidenced (T2.7.1–T2.7.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Body-characteristic links and their directionality are evidenced (T2.7.1–T2.7.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Body-characteristic links and their bidirectionality are evidenced (T2.7.1–T2.7.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Body-characteristic links and their directionality are evidenced (T2.7.1–T2.7.2). This prompt is satisfied.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Body-characteristic link and directionality are evidenced (T2.7.1–T2.7.2). This prompt is satisfied.

---

#### T2.8 — Body — Deposit

##### T2.8.1 — Does sustained operation of this characteristic leave a constitutional deposit in the body or its design — including DNA or generational consequence?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The evidence surfaces two forms of sustained-operation deposit. (1) Social-structural deposit: wickedness becomes institutionally embedded — Hab 1:4 (VCG-03): "the wicked surround the righteous; so justice goes forth perverted" — the wicked's sustained operation reshapes the structural environment so that justice is systematically distorted. (2) Self-reinforcing bondage: Pro 5:22 (VCG-06) — "the iniquities of the wicked ensnare him, and he is held fast in the cords of his sin" — the sustained operation of wickedness produces a material-metaphorical constitutional deposit in the form of self-generated bondage. (3) Generational transmission: Num 16:26 (VCG-04) — "touch nothing of theirs, lest you be swept away with all their sins" — the sustained operation of wickedness in a community (Korah's men) creates a contagious-dangerous deposit that threatens proximity; the verse implies generational/communal consequence. The evidence is not explicit about DNA-level or generational biological deposit.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The evidence surfaces two forms of sustained-operation deposit. (1) Self-reinforcing progressive deterioration: 2Ti 3:13 (vc=14451 — VCG-06): "evil people and impostors will go on from bad to worse" — the characteristic's sustained operation produces a deepening deposit of moral corruption in the person's trajectory. (2) Expanding inner occupation: Mat 12:45 (vc=65879 — VCG-06): the vacated inner space refilled with "seven other spirits more evil than itself" — sustained and then worsened inner occupation; the last state is worse than the first. (3) The spreading-leaven dynamic: 1Cor 5:8 (vc=14363/14412 — VCG-05): kakia and ponēria as old leaven — the leaven metaphor implies that the deposit spreads and corrupts over time, progressively affecting more of the whole. The evidence does not specifically address DNA-level or generational biological deposit.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The evidence documents a conscience-level deposit. Jer 6:15 (vc=1680 — VCG-04) and Jer 8:12 (vc=1696 — VCG-04) show a state where sustained commission of abomination has produced a permanently silenced conscience — the faculty that should produce shame "did not know how to blush." The sustained deposit is the functional elimination of the conscience's shame-producing capacity. Eze 44:13 (vc=66003 — VCG-04) shows a different deposit: the abominations "that they have committed" become a permanent weight of shame they "shall bear" — the abominations are retained as a personal burden. Ezr 9:11 (vc=66005 — VCG-04): abominations filling the land "from end to end" shows a communal-environmental deposit through which the moral contamination becomes embedded in shared space. The primary individual deposit is the silenced conscience; the secondary communal deposit is the saturating moral contamination of shared space.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Yes. The evidence documents two forms of sustained deposit. (1) Constitutional character-transformation: Hos 9:10 (vc=1632 — VCG-04): "they became detestable like the thing they loved" — sustained idolatrous devotion deposits a transformed character in the person, making them in inner being what the idol is. This is a constitutional deposit in the deepest sense: the inner character is re-shaped by what it worships. (2) Land defilement as collective-environmental deposit: Eze 33:29 (vc=65999 — VCG-05): "the land a desolation and a waste because of all their abominations"; Jer 16:18 (vc=65964 — VCG-04): "have filled my inheritance with their abominations" — the sustained collective idolatrous abomination deposits a moral-spiritual defilement in the shared environment, creating a legacy that shapes subsequent generations.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The evidence documents a conscience-deposit and a moral-trajectory deposit. (1) Conscience deadening: Pro 30:20 (vc=38222 — VCG-04): the adulteress who wipes her mouth and says "I have done no wrong" — sustained commission of iniquity without arrest has entirely silenced the conscience; the inner moral faculty no longer registers the wrongdoing. This is a conscience-capacity deposit: the repeated commission deposits a progressive insensitivity. (2) The worn inner path: Job 22:15 (vc=38210 — VCG-04): "the old way that wicked men have trod" — sustained practice of iniquity deposits a worn inner trajectory — a habitual moral path that becomes the default direction. (3) Iniquity's dominion as sustained deposit: Psa 119:133 (vc=38227 — VCG-04): iniquity seeking "dominion" — the sustained inner presence of iniquity accumulates toward gaining controlling influence over the will.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

The evidence documents a will-hardening deposit. Rev 16:9 → 16:11 → 16:21 (VCG-01): across three separate escalating divine judgments, the inner posture intensifies rather than yields — each judgment compounds the defiance rather than breaking it. The sustained operation of the characteristic deposits a progressive hardening of the will against both God and the possibility of repentance. Rev 16:11 (vc=14350 — VCG-01): "they did not repent of their deeds" — not repenting of deeds is the inner evidence of the deposit: the sustained characteristic has produced a will that can no longer orient itself toward repentance even under maximum pressure.

---

##### T2.8.2 — What evidence supports or contradicts this?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

Supporting deposit: Pro 5:22 (self-generated bondage), Num 16:26 (contagious community-level consequence), Hab 1:4 (structural perversion of justice), Eze 7:21 (VCG-03 — the wicked as instruments of profanation in God's judgment — the deposit is that they become instruments of his judgment, affecting others beyond themselves). Contra-deposit (or limiting the deposit): Eze 18:20 (VCG-07) explicitly limits generational deposit — "the son shall not suffer for the iniquity of the father, nor the father suffer for the iniquity of the son; the wickedness of the wicked shall be upon himself" — this is a theologically significant limit on the deposit concept. The evidence thus presents both a social-structural deposit and an individual-moral-accountability constraint on that deposit.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

Supporting deposit: 2Ti 3:13 (progressive deterioration), Mat 12:45 (deepening inner occupation), 1Cor 5:8 (spreading leaven). The spreading-leaven metaphor is particularly significant: leaven in its original context means the corruption spreads through the whole batch — the deposit expands. The community-level spread is evidenced in 1Cor 5:6 (cited by context of 1Cor 5:8 — "a little leaven leavens the whole lump"). The individual deposit is the progressively deteriorating constitutional state. Contra-deposit or limiting evidence: the evidence for reversal (Act 3:26 — VCG-05: turning from wickedness; Heb 10:22 — VCG-06: hearts sprinkled clean from an evil conscience; Tit 3:3-4: former malice replaced through grace) shows the deposit is not fixed or deterministic — it can be addressed by divine intervention. The deposit is real but not permanently binding.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Supporting deposit: Jer 6:15; 8:12 (VCG-04 — conscience wholly silenced as sustained deposit), Eze 44:13 (VCG-04 — abominations as permanent weight), Ezr 9:11 (VCG-04 — communal saturation). Contradicting (or limiting) the permanence of the deposit: Eze 36:31 (vc=1681 — VCG-04): "you will remember your evil ways… and will loathe yourselves for your iniquities and your abominations" — the memory of abominations and the self-loathing conscience can be restored through divine action; Eze 14:6 (vc=65984 — VCG-04): "repent and turn away from your idols" — the call to repentance shows the conscience-deposit is not permanently fixed. Act 3:26 context (from CHAR-2's corpus) is not in this evidence base — within CHAR-3's 40 verses, the limiting evidence is the Ezekiel repentance/restoration passages. The deposit is real and serious but not deterministically fixed.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Supporting deposit: Hos 9:10 (VCG-04 — constitutional character transformation), Jer 16:18 (VCG-04 — land filled with abominations), Eze 33:29 (VCG-05 — desolation as consequence of accumulated abominations), Eze 20:4 (vc=65994 — VCG-05 — "abominations of their fathers" as a legacy requiring confrontation). Contra-deposit (limiting): Eze 37:23 (vc=65913 — VCG-05): divine cleansing removes the deposit — "I will save them from all the backslidings in which they have sinned, and will cleanse them" — the deposit is real but not permanently fixed; divine intervention can remove it. The deposit is serious and generationally significant but not absolutely irreversible.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Supporting deposit: Pro 30:20 (VCG-04 — conscience silenced as deposit), Job 22:15 (VCG-04 — worn path as deposit), Psa 119:133 (VCG-04 — dominion-seeking as deposit), Psa 36:12 (vc=38233 — VCG-04 — irrecoverable collapse as terminus of the deposit trajectory). Contra-deposit: Job 36:10 (vc=38215 — VCG-04): "He opens their ears to instruction and commands that they return from iniquity" — divine action can reverse the trajectory; Job 11:14 (vc=38207 — VCG-04): "put it far away" — the call to remove iniquity implies the deposit is not permanently fixed; Jer 4:14 (vc=38205 — VCG-02): "wash your heart from evil" — the washing-command implies reversibility. The deposit is real and progressive but remains reversible through divine action and volitional response.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Supporting deposit: Rev 16:9/11/21 (VCG-01 — escalating hardening across three plagues); Jude 8 (vc=14354 — VCG-01: dreamers who have already settled into their authority-rejecting posture). Contradicting or limiting: 1Pe 2:12 (vc=14377 — VCG-03): the false accusers who will "see your good deeds and glorify God on the day of visitation" — this implies the possibility of reversal for at least some false accusers; the deposit for VCG-03 false accusation is less absolute than for VCG-01 hardened blasphemy. The deposit is most clearly evidenced for the hardened-will VCG-01 blasphemy; VCG-02/03 false accusation may be more reversible.

---

##### T2.8.3 — If the evidence is silent, note this explicitly. This finding feeds directly into T5.7.

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The evidence is not silent; deposits are evidenced with both supporting and limiting data (T2.8.1–T2.8.2). The primary constitutional deposit identified is the self-reinforcing bondage of Pro 5:22 and the structural consequence of Hab 1:4. This feeds into T5.7.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The evidence is not silent on deposit; T2.8.1–T2.8.2 identify and analyse it. This feeds directly into T5.7.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The evidence is not silent on deposit (T2.8.1–T2.8.2). This feeds directly into T5.7.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The evidence is not silent on deposit (T2.8.1–T2.8.2). This feeds directly into T5.7.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The evidence is not silent on deposit (T2.8.1–T2.8.2). This feeds directly into T5.7.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

The evidence is not silent on deposit (T2.8.1–T2.8.2). This feeds directly into T5.7.

---

#### T2.9 — Origin and Source

##### T2.9.1 — Where does this characteristic originate constitutionally — is it generated from within the person, received from outside, bestowed by God, or carried generationally?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The evidence presents wickedness-as-settled-person-identity as generated from within the person — not primarily received from outside. The inner-voice model (Psa 36:1: "transgression speaks to the wicked deep in his heart") places the origin within the heart's own self-governance structure. 1Sa 24:13 ("out of the wicked comes wickedness") is the canonical origin-statement: the wicked person is the generative source of their own wickedness. Pro 4:14 (VCG-07: "do not enter the path of the wicked") frames the characteristic as entered by a volitional choice — but once entered, the evidence shows it becomes self-generating. The practical atheism cluster (VCG-02) roots the origin in the decision to exclude God: the wicked person's thoughts are organised around "There is no God" (Psa 10:4) — an internal disposition produced by a prior volitional act of God-exclusion.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The evidence presents the characteristic as originating from within the person — as the constitutional baseline of human inner nature. Mat 7:11 (vc=14438 — VCG-02): "you who are evil" addresses humans collectively as constitutionally evil — this is a baseline statement about human inner nature as a whole, not a description of particular acquired vices. Luk 11:13 (vc=14445 — VCG-02) is the parallel: "you who are evil" — constitutional. Mar 7:23 (vc=14422 — VCG-03): "all these evil things come from within" — the within is the origin. The evidence does not address the developmental or theological origin of why human inner nature is constitutionally evil (that belongs to the sin/fall discussion outside this cluster) — it describes the constitutional state as the given condition from which the characteristic operates.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The evidence presents abomination-as-inner-condition as originating from within the person's own moral character — specifically from the heart's orientation (crooked, arrogant) and the will's choices. Pro 11:20 (vc=1677 — VCG-01): the crooked heart is the origin of the abominable status. Pro 16:5 (vc=1689 — VCG-02): arrogance in heart is self-generated. Deu 27:15 (vc=65937 — VCG-04): the person "makes" and "sets up" the idol in secret — the act originates from within their volitional choice while their inner moral knowledge knows it is wrong. The characteristic does not originate as something bestowed from outside but as a quality that develops from the inner moral conditions the person cultivates or allows to develop.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The evidence presents idolatrous abomination as originating from a combination of inner volitional choice and environmental-relational influence. Inner volitional choice: Isa 66:3 (vc=1633 — VCG-04): "they have chosen their own ways" — the volitional choice is the constitutional origin-point. Environmental-relational origin: Deu 7:25 (vc=1682 — VCG-02): coveting what is on the idols; Deu 20:18 (vc=65932 — VCG-02): the nations "may teach you to do according to all their abominable practices" — external influence as the channel through which the characteristic enters. The combination is: a volitional capacity for devotion that is attracted by external idol-objects (their beauty, their material — Eze 7:20: ornament used for idols) and makes a choice to attach itself to them rather than to God.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The evidence presents iniquity as active scheming as originating from within the person's own inner generative faculties — heart, mind, and will. Psa 7:14 (vc=38245 — VCG-02): "the wicked man conceives evil" — the origin is internal; the wicked person's own inner life is the generative source. Isa 32:6 (vc=38181 — VCG-02): "his heart is busy with iniquity" — the heart's own busyness is the origin. Job 15:35 (vc=38208 — VCG-02): "their womb prepares deceit" — the inner womb as the generative source. The characteristic is self-generated from within rather than received from outside, distinguishing it from characteristics that originate through external influence.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

The evidence presents the characteristic as originating from within the person's own volitional and moral faculties. Jude 8 (vc=14354 — VCG-01): "relying on their dreams, they defile the flesh, reject authority, and blaspheme the glorious ones" — the origin is the inner volitional sequence: sensory self-reliance (dreams) → wilful authority-rejection → blasphemy. Rev 16:9/11/21 (VCG-01): the origin is the hardened will refusing to repent even under maximum pressure. Rom 2:24 (vc=14357 — VCG-02): the origin is the moral failure of those who claim to represent God — the inner moral state of the speaker produces the social defamation of God's name. The characteristic originates within the person's own will and moral character, not as a received external condition.

---

##### T2.9.2 — What does the evidence reveal about whether the origin is singular or multiple?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The evidence presents multiple contributing origins rather than a single point. Pride appears as a root: Pro 21:4 (VCG-03) names "haughty eyes and a proud heart" as the lamp of the wicked — pride is an originating inner attitude. The exclusion of God (VCG-02) is another originating event. Social alignment with the wicked (Psa 1:1 — "walks in the counsel of the wicked") contributes as an external-becoming-internal origin. Job 34:8 (re.sha, VCG-11) notes that "walking in company with evildoers" reflects a chosen inner alignment — social context becomes a contributory origin. The evidence thus presents a multiple-origin picture: pride, God-exclusion, chosen volitional direction, and social-moral alignment all contribute to the settling of this characteristic.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The evidence presents the origin as the singular constitutional condition of human inner nature (the "you who are evil" baseline of Mat 7:11 and Luk 11:13 — VCG-02). However, the VCG-05 saturation cluster (Rom 1:29 — VCG-05: "filled with all manner of unrighteousness, evil, covetousness, malice") shows the constitutional condition producing multiple specific vices — the singular constitutional evil generates a multiplicity of specific expressions. The relationship is one origin (the constitutional condition) producing multiple expressions (the vice catalogue). Additionally, VCG-01's cosmic-evil dimension (the evil one's domain — 1Jo 5:19: "the whole world lies in the power of the evil one") introduces a supra-personal source that is external to the individual but operative in the environment that shapes the constitutionally evil person.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The evidence presents multiple originating inner conditions. The VCG structure itself maps multiple: pride/arrogance in heart (VCG-02), dishonest practice revealing a character of fraud (VCG-01), the corrupt inner person's religious approach (VCG-03), conscience silencing (VCG-04), and the identity constituted by abomination (VCG-05). Pro 26:25 (vc=1694 — VCG-02): "seven abominations in his heart" — the very plurality (seven) suggests multiple concurrent originating conditions within the same person. Pro 6:16 (vc=65952 — VCG-05): "six things that the Lord hates, seven that are an abomination" — the listing implies multiple distinct origins for the abominable category, not a single root. The origin is thus multiple: various specific inner conditions each qualify as originating sources of abomination.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The evidence presents multiple originating pathways: (1) pride perverting gifts into idols (Eze 7:20 — vc=65909/65975 — VCG-05: pride as the internal mechanism); (2) coveting what is on the idols (Deu 7:25 — VCG-02: desire/covetousness as the entry mechanism); (3) marital-relational entanglement with idolaters (Ezr 9:1; 9:14 — VCG-03: relational influence); (4) royal institutionalization (VCG-03 — kings who install abominations, leading communities into them by authority); (5) inherited patterns from ancestors (Eze 20:4 — VCG-05: "abominations of their fathers"). The origin is thus multiple: pride, covetousness, relational entanglement, royal authority, and generational inheritance all appear as originating pathways.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The evidence presents multiple originating inner faculties working together: the heart (Isa 32:6 — VCG-02 — busy), the thought-life (Isa 59:7 — VCG-02 — thoughts of iniquity), and the will (Job 36:21 — VCG-04 — chosen rather than affliction). These are not three separate origins but three facets of the same inner generative process. Additionally, relational-social influence appears as a secondary originating channel: Job 34:8 (vc=38214 — VCG-04): "travels in company with evildoers" — chosen association with evildoers shapes the inner person toward iniquity. The origin is primarily internal and multiple (heart + mind + will in conjunction) with a secondary social-relational influence pathway.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

The evidence presents multiple originating conditions, varying by VCG. VCG-01: the origin is the hardened will combined with authority-rejection and cognitive incomprehension (Jude 8: authority-rejection + sensory indulgence; Jude 10: incomprehension + contempt). VCG-02: the origin is moral failure (Rom 2:24), false attribution (Rom 3:8), misuse of freedom (Rom 14:16; 1Cor 10:30), or received slander's social consequence (1Cor 4:13). VCG-03: the origin is malicious hostile evaluation (Joh 18:30) or civil-legal process wrongdoing (Act 25:5; 1Pe 2:14). The origin is thus multiple and varies by register — from the hardened-will's authority-rejection (VCG-01) to hostile social judgment (VCG-03) to moral failure enabling defamation (VCG-02).

---

##### T2.9.3 — Does the origin of this characteristic change across different contexts evidenced in Scripture?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The evidence does not show a radically different origin across different scriptural contexts, but the emphasis varies. In the Psalms (VCG-02, 03, 05), the origin emphasis is on the inner God-exclusion and pride. In Proverbs (VCG-06, 07, 08, 09), the emphasis is on volitional path-choice and the characteristic's self-generating momentum once entered. In Ezekiel (VCG-07), the focus is on the characteristic as a directional commitment of the will that can be reversed — here the origin is less in view than the possibility of departure. In Job (VCG-10), the characteristic is examined in the context of theodicy — its origin is not the focus but its persistence and apparent prosperity. The origin-picture is consistent across contexts but its emphasis shifts between the dispositional-constitutional (Psalms) and the volitional-directional (Proverbs, Ezekiel).

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The evidence does not show a changed origin across contexts, but the emphasis varies. In the Synoptic corpus (VCGs 02 and 03), the origin emphasis is the constitutional baseline of human inner nature (Mat 7:11; Luk 11:13) and the heart as generative source (Mat 12:34-35; Mar 7:23). In the Pauline corpus (VCG-05 — adikia/kakia/ponēria), the emphasis is on the saturating accumulation of multiple vice-expressions of the constitutional evil (Rom 1:29 — "filled with all manner"). In the Johannine corpus (VCG-01 — the evil one's domain), the origin emphasis shifts to the cosmic framing: the world under the evil one's power (1Jo 5:19). The constitutional origin is consistent across contexts; the framing of how that constitution relates to cosmic, social, and individual dimensions varies.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The origin emphasis varies by context but the constitutional core remains consistent. In Proverbs (VCGs 01, 02, 03): the origin is firmly in specific inner-being conditions — the crooked heart, the arrogant heart, the thoughts, the will choosing dishonest practice. In the Prophets (VCGs 04, partial 05): the origin emphasis shifts to the communal dimension — the abominations of a people (Eze 44:6-7; Ezr 9:11; Jer 6:15; 8:12) and their conscience-silencing trajectory. In the NT (VCG-02 bdelugma/bdeluktos; VCG-05): the origin returns to the individual inner dimension — the self-justifying heart (Luk 16:15), the knowledge-works disconnect (Tit 1:16). The origin is consistently within the inner person across contexts; what changes is whether it is primarily individual-character (Proverbs, NT) or communal-trajectory (Prophets).

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The originating emphasis varies by context. In Deuteronomy (VCG-02): origin is relational exposure — proximity to idolatrous peoples is the primary hazard (Deu 20:18; 18:9). In the historical narratives (VCG-03): origin is royal volition — the king's will (Solomon's relational entanglements, Manasseh's comprehensive adoption of pagan practices) is the gateway. In Ezekiel (VCG-05): origin is the accumulated inner heart-attachment — "heart goes after detestable things" as a sustained directional movement. In the Prophets (VCG-04): origin is stubborn inner refusal to heed prophetic correction — stubbornness perpetuating what began from other origins. The origin pattern is consistent (inner volitional attachment + external influence) but its primary emphasis varies by the distinctive context of each VCG.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The constitutional origin (heart-mind-will) is consistent across all contexts. What varies by context is the emphasis: Deuteronomy/Jeremiah (VCG-05) emphasises the heart as the origin of evil deeds (Jer 4:4 — VCG-05: "evil deeds from uncircumcised heart"); Proverbs (VCG-02/03) emphasises the cognitive-devising mode (Pro 6:18 — VCG-02: heart devising wicked plans); Psalms (VCG-03/04) emphasises the accumulation and storage mode (Psa 66:18 — VCG-04: cherished in heart; Psa 41:6 — VCG-04: heart gathers iniquity); the prophets (VCG-02) emphasise the nocturnal-planning mode (Mic 2:1; Psa 36:4). The inner-constitutional origin is consistent; the mode of generation varies by context.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Yes. VCG-01 (apocalyptic/prophetic contexts): the origin is eschatological hardened will under maximum judgment — a uniquely extreme context of origin. Jude 8/10 (epistolary): the origin is false spiritual-charismatic experience ("relying on their dreams") combined with antinomian self-indulgence — a community context. VCG-02 (Pauline epistolary): the origin varies from community conduct-failure (Rom 2:24) to intra-community disputes about freedom (Rom 14:16; 1Cor 10:30). VCG-03 (narrative and Petrine epistolary): the origin is hostile social-legal accusation of minority communities (1Pe 2:12/3:16) or judicial narrative (Joh 18:30). The constitutional origin (inner will/moral character) is consistent; the contextual triggering conditions vary significantly by literary and social context.

---

#### T2.10 — Constitutional Movement

##### T2.10.1 — Does this characteristic move across constitutional levels — from spirit to soul, from soul to body, or across boundaries in other directions?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

Yes. The primary movement evidenced is from the inner constitutional levels (heart, soul) outward to the body (mouth, arm) and to the social/structural level (VCG-08 speech-based social destruction; VCG-03 directed hostility as physically enacted harm). The soul-to-body movement is documented at T2.7.1. There is also a movement from the individual inner level to the social-structural level: Pro 11:11 ("by the mouth of the wicked a city is overthrown"), Hab 1:4 (justice structurally perverted), Hab 3:13 (VCG-03 — "the house of the wicked" as an institutional wickedness structure). The characteristic does not appear to move from body back to spirit in the evidence — the movement is outward from the constitutional interior to the social and physical exterior.

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

Yes. The movement evidenced is from the heart/inner constitutional level outward to the body and social sphere. Mat 12:34-35 (vc=14419-14420 — VCG-03): heart → mouth → social impact. Mar 7:23 (vc=14422 — VCG-03): from within → defiling the person → outward expression. Mat 6:23 (vc=14458 — VCG-03): the bad eye floods "the whole body" — the movement is from the eye (inner perceptive faculty) to the whole body. Rom 6:13 (vc=14340 — VCG-06): inner unrighteousness → body members as instruments → outward acts. The movement is consistently centrifugal: from the heart/conscience/mind (inner) through the body's instruments (expressive) to the social/relational sphere (consequential). No movement from body back to soul is evidenced as a primary pattern.

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

Yes. The evidence documents movement from inner constitutional levels outward to expression and communal space. At the individual level: inner heart condition (crooked heart, arrogant heart — VCG-02) → outward expression in practice (dishonest commerce — VCG-01) and speech (lying lips — VCG-02) → worship act (corrupt sacrifice — VCG-03) → social/communal impact (saturating the land — Ezr 9:11 — VCG-04). At the worship level: inner person's corrupt state (Pro 15:8 — VCG-03) → the offered sacrifice or prayer → divine revulsion verdict. The characteristic also moves through the conscience: inner act of abomination → conscience registration (or non-registration — VCG-04) → shame response (or absence). The movement is outward and communal, from constitutional inner condition to social and sacred-space consequences.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

Yes. The movement is multidirectional. Primary inner-to-outer: soul and heart attachment → eyes feasting → hands crafting → idols installed in sacred space → land defiled (Eze 7:20 — VCG-05 — ornament to idol; Jer 16:18 — VCG-04 — land filled with abominations; Lev 18:27 — VCG-01 — land made unclean). The constitutional movement goes from the deepest inner levels (soul delight, heart going after) through the perceptive-desire level (eyes feasting) to the bodily-enacted level (hands crafting, feet going to high places) to the communal-environmental level (land defilement). Secondary outer-to-inner feedback: the installed idols reinforce the inner attachment (T2.7.1). The characteristic moves comprehensively from within to without, with feedback from the outer to reinforce the inner.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

Yes. The movement is consistently inner-to-outer. The constitutional sequence runs: heart-and-mind (deepest inner — scheming and conceiving) → tongue/speech (inner-expressive bridge) → hand-and-feet (bodily enactment) → social-communal harm (external impact on victims). Mic 2:1 (vc=38217 — VCG-02): nocturnal devising (inner-cognitive) → dawn performance (bodily-social). Isa 59:7 (vc=38203 — VCG-02): thoughts of iniquity (cognitive-inner) → feet run to evil (bodily-directional) → innocent blood shed (social harm). Psa 28:3 (vc=38232 — VCG-03): evil in hearts (inner) → speech of peace (expressive-outer) → social deception (relational harm). The movement is consistently from deep constitutional inner through the expressive levels to social-communal impact.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

Yes. The movement is consistently inner-to-outer and bottom-to-top. The sequence: inner will-orientation (hardened refusal to repent — Rev 16:9 — VCG-01; authority-rejection — Jude 8 — VCG-01) → volitional choice to open the mouth (Rev 13:6 — VCG-01: "opened its mouth") → speech act through the mouth → social-relational impact (God's name dishonoured among Gentiles — Rom 2:24 — VCG-02; false accusation of the innocent — Joh 18:30 — VCG-03). The movement crosses from the deepest will level through the speech instrument to the social-communal level.

---

##### T2.10.2 — What does the evidence reveal about the sequence or pattern of that movement?

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

The pattern is centrifugal: from the innermost constitutional location (heart, soul — the wickedness voice of Psa 36:1; the soul-desire of Pro 21:10) outward through the body's instruments (mouth, arm — VCG-08; VCG-03) to social and structural space (community destruction, institutional perversion of justice — Hab 1:4; Pro 11:11). The sequence is: inner disposition → volitional orientation ("way" — VCG-07) → behavioural expression (speech, physical harm — VCGs 03, 08) → structural consequence (social/institutional corruption — VCG-03, Hab 1:4). This centrifugal movement explains why the wicked person's wickedness affects others and communities, not only themselves — the movement of the characteristic outward is constitutive of its social dangerousness (Num 16:26 — the contagious-sweeping-away risk).

**[CHAR-2] Evil as constitutional inner nature** (E)

The pattern is consistently: constitutional inner condition (heart/conscience/mind as evil) → expressive body instrument (mouth/eye/members) → outward social consequence (community harm, relational defiling, legal offense). Mat 12:34 (VCG-03) states this sequence explicitly: heart abundance → mouth speech. Luk 6:45 (VCG-03): evil heart-treasure → evil output through speech. Mat 6:23 (VCG-03): bad eye → whole-body darkness. This sequential pattern reveals the characteristic as a generative pipeline: the constitutional evil inner state is the engine; the body's instruments are the transmission channels; the outward social world is where the characteristic's damage lands. The pattern is not circular (body back to heart) but unidirectional (heart to world).

**[CHAR-3] Abomination — divine revulsion on moral character** (E)

The pattern is: inner character condition (heart) → volitional expression in practice or speech → divine revulsion verdict → conscience response (shame/grief or silence). The key divergence in the pattern occurs at the conscience-response stage: when conscience is functional (Eze 9:4 — VCG-04), the sequence produces shame and grief that can initiate repentance. When conscience is silenced (Jer 6:15; 8:12 — VCG-04), the sequence produces abomination → divine judgment without inner braking. The communal trajectory follows the individual pattern at scale: individual inner abomination → communal practice → saturation of shared space (Ezr 9:11 — VCG-04: "filled it from end to end"). The sequence is not primarily cognitive but moral-relational: the inner condition → the violated sacred boundary → the divine response.

**[CHAR-4] Idolatrous abomination** (E)

The pattern is: inner volitional-devotional choice (will choosing the idol's way — Isa 66:3: "chosen their own ways") → heart and soul attachment (Eze 11:21 — heart going after; Isa 66:3 — soul delighting) → perceptive-desire feeding (Eze 20:7 — eyes feasting) → bodily enactment (crafting idols — Eze 7:20; installing them in sacred space — Jer 7:30) → communal-environmental defilement (land filled — Jer 16:18; Lev 18:27) → divine-presence withdrawal (Eze 5:11 — VCG-05) → eventual divine judgment and desolation (Eze 33:29 — VCG-05). The sequence reveals the characteristic as a comprehensive trajectory from inner choice to cosmic consequence.

**[CHAR-5] Iniquity as active inner scheming and evil generation** (E)

The pattern is: inner cognitive devising (heart-busy, thoughts of iniquity) → sub-lingual positioning for speech deployment (under the tongue — Psa 10:7 — VCG-04) → outward expression through speech, hand, or feet → social-communal harm (eating up the people — Psa 14:4 — VCG-03; dropping trouble on victims — Psa 55:3 — VCG-01; filling the community — Psa 55:10 — VCG-01). The sequence is also generational: Job 21:19 (vc=38209 — VCG-04): "God stores up their iniquity for their children" — the iniquity accumulated in one generation is deferred to the next. The full constitutional movement is from the deepest inner generative level through expressive levels to social and generational impact.

**[CHAR-6] Evil expressed through speech** (E)

The pattern is: inner will-state (hardened defiance / authority-rejection / moral failure) → deliberate volitional choice of the speech act (opening the mouth — Rev 13:6 — VCG-01) → speech act (cursing, blaspheming, falsely accusing) → social-relational impact (dishonour to God's name — Rom 2:24 — VCG-02; injury to persons' reputations — 1Cor 4:13 — VCG-02; false charge against the innocent — Joh 18:30 — VCG-03). The key constitutional transition is at the will-to-mouth junction: the deliberate opening of the mouth (Rev 13:6 — VCG-01) is the decisive inner-outer crossover that makes the characteristic socially operative. The sequence is irreversible in the moment of utterance — once spoken, the blasphemy or false charge has social reality regardless of subsequent inner state.

---

##### T2.10.3 — If no constitutional movement is evidenced, note this explicitly.

**[CHAR-1] Wickedness as settled person-identity** (E)

Constitutional movement is evidenced (T2.10.1–T2.10.2). This prompt is satisfied.
